- Nihiltheism is characterized by several key refusals, including not being a simple negation of meaning, not asserting the existence of external deities, not being a form of passive resignation, not seeking to escape existential reality through metaphysical constructs, not developing in isolation from other philosophical traditions, not being a fixed set of beliefs, and not being purely individual in its approach to meaning-creation.
